gratulation argument present gladnes yf remorce shame reputacion honor hadde bene impedimentes desyer harte cloasinge mouth againste present conceytes ioye newe societie immediatlye dismissed messenger absolute assurance performe request sent hym wherof albeit shame seamed abridge expedicion offer cause staye time yet wantynge force mortifye altogether humour ragyng desyer driuen gyue place prouocation loue deuestinge honest shamfastnes whiche oughte chiefe habite decoracion beautie greate ladyes willed deferre lenger thynge alredye vowed seynge ye iniurie present tyme denied satisfye hym woulde leaste yelde hym suche contentement maye wherfore takynge pen ynke paper replied letter wyth aunswere circumstaunce present letter syr seames plaudyna aunsvvereth letter seruant argue excepcion frendly lookes glaunces mine eye wherin albeit could note great simplicitie want discrecion constreth regardes ladye cast vnwares commoditye hymselfe wynninge good meaneth nothing lesse make minister loue yet beinge ready content therin curious mine owne behauiour acquite imputacion waye couert ye note ye follie ouersight selfe albeit pleasant encounter mine eys seaming liberal behalf familiaritie ordinarie al men may persuade certein differece haue put betwen frendship respect desyer embrace aboue one creature yet opinio sondrye vertues reputation honor would suffer chalenge firste faulte conuerte theis regardes simple colde fauor suche consequence attempte violation mine honor grudgeth lose vowe faith husbande forbiddes depart withall notwithstanding yelde lesse thankes curtesye seame gyue commendacion beautye giftes note accomptinge greater price value estimacion make neither wil refuse ye proffer present frendship hope voyde intent preiudice mine honor let suffise contented admit fauor also determined hold lesse deare tendrest part selfe letter incident manye casualty commonly fyrst discloasers secretes louers aduise hensfurth staye diligence pen absent cornelio preferred vehement desyer onely recouer hym wherin appcared greate impossibilitye also wishinge bee companyon iorney partaker miserye seamed expose franke whiche earste ash amed made theis tearmes thinges ought hatefull eares seame hurteful quiet mynde yet one chiefe consolation plaudina menteth absence fred vvith complaint gainste ovvne misfortune wee fynde miserye recorde circunstaunce misfortune neither grief greate importance whose cause small moment ala sorow semblable separacion frendes ah cornelio auncient grudge procureth newe mislike offence haue late make husband allowed greately honest diligence hys wyfe blamed altogether thabuse capteyne whome threatened requyte semblable curtesye wherin dowted nothing tractable nature simple husbande beyng glad notwithstandyng haue smothly appeased humor iust anger accompted selfe neyther free cause feare quite deliuered distresse till made meane manifest comming husbande louer chymneye knew passed feare frencheme dowting wold dread daunger discende ymediatly frozen mewe toke goodman hand led hym place place watche lefte al thynges oute order bringing hym last chamber cornelio stoode like crowe gutter castell cage small ease yt pennance indured seamed rather excede haynous respect offece sufficient punishement falte beyng desyer vyolacion act yet veraye voice husbande restored hym suche treble countenance mighte haue auowched infydell vttermost ilandes tartaria whych brought sely freare suche mortall perplexitie dispaire beganne appeare wyth thapproche sondrye perentorie disease chiefly yt hyer earnest loue retorned sondry sort crueltye disdainefull repulse occupyinge brayne suche contrarietie thoughtes voide councell saint vow himselfe vpon wood make arrowes seinge neither hable mortifye vse moderacion passion muche lesse assisted meane communicate greatnes greefe whose beautie made hym slaue follie wherein albeit sawe vanitie vse office dariolleta bawde vertue maide argued detestation suche embassador write appeared great difficultie alwayes presence mother vsinge vertue doughter solace olde yeres lesse carefull honestie longed precious iewell yet felinge continuall aggrauation desyer wyth flatterynge offer loue rewarde hym ende praye purseute determined suborne shameles messenger bewraye shameful intente therefore put requeste vpon tearmes letter effecte yf destenies execution abbot vvriteth mistres vppon bodie firste brought viewe beautie ben presente experience crueltye thoccasion vnworthie torment death nature preuented begynnynge loue ben free force passion discharged mortall greefe dispensed al imputation cause double ill one abuse vertue selfe wronge renowme al woman preferring effectes rigour disdaynyng seruice whose life death payseth indifferentlye ballaunce good dissemblynge also see circunstaunce loue driue desperacion point vse vnnaturall force againste selfe howe often ala haue made priuye thinwarde affection mynde outwarde regardes glaunces exterior partes howe often haue acknowledged argument semblable glee immediatly denied whole soddaine showe angrie complexion eyther disdayning vtterly thoffer seruice one vnworthie enioye preferment fauor dalyenge wyth earnest sute geue increase passion haue often bene vpon waye disclose vnto mouth thinge wherin hart hath alreadie geuen iudgmente meaning albeit desier offende waye hath staide thexpedicion intent suspendyng grefe till greatnes hath forced presente vente wt simple requeste fearinge ymparte full great matter vncerteine messenger pece paper may please geue credit coferece wher selues may witness whych haue discouer longer hable conceile wherin ther bonde consideracion great ladyes behalf offer inferiours ymagin iustly deserue well wyth reason oughte passe graunte small fauor hym lesse hable know procure aduancement wyth porcion wealthe selfe shall thinke good readye performe thinges shall ymagyn wishe wherof sende confirmacion herewith sealed othe religion protestacion faythe life moste loyall desolate seruante gonsaldo soner written letter mynde eftsones commit morsells make sacrafice fyer dispairing belike successe till laste blind guide fyrst author follie reprehendinge want corage renforced hym forwardnes perswading loue hym beginning good argued sequeile contentacion rather saieth tender yeres wyth small discrecion preferreth ignorance girle meaning seing accesse conference denied yt next pollicie vse thaduantage writinge whyche declareth theffect whyche painted outwarde regardes face wordes letter may also importe charme present rigour may conuerted spedie copassion conning enchau tyng misterie wrought without assistaunce word foolishe suggestion restored abbot hope makyng conscience committ conueigh creditt anye couent doubted wisdome performinge secret embassage vsed thexpedicion one vallettes chamber put remembraunce thauncient fauours vsed behalfe howe much reaposed hymself assurance fidelitie said nowe imploye fayth diligence busynes lesse value price life wherin sayeth albeit thou maiest conster part meaning circustaunce late chaunge alteracio thou haste noted iudgyng peraduenture procede amarous humour yet althoughe consente make good conceite thy fancie surmise thow deuinours worlde name thou seest hath made flaue beautie secret wherin make last experience thy indeuour wisedome make presente theis letterrs hath yet vouchesaffed lende vse one simple regarde fauor qualifye heate burnynge martyrdom wherewith told name mistres streete signe wher father dwelte straite commaundement ende omitt remembraunce theyr venemous basilike wyth woordes oppen infamye companye euer bothe intisynge meanes hadde traine menne lure wyth subteltyes shee dismyssed theyme beynge wearye companye sawe offer hath nothyng suche hardnes dare attempte thinge greate impossibilitye whiche wyll appeare easye pursuete trauell maye receiue hyer hades bountye pardon beseche discoueryng whiche almost kepte secret mine owne harte yf rashenes haue offended maye lyke iustice vpon selfe whose authoritie force extreme passion hath forced lauishenes thyng whiche durste determyne muche lesse seeke set abroche deede shameles lady tolde last request preuented longe meaninge saith haue hyt marke whereat thoughte shoote wherein cotented imparte credit wordes wt persuacio sufficient assurauce fidelitye praye embrace place comitt hys bodie sacrafy ce ransome fauour moueth ala discreditt doute payne wyth opynion passion dyssembled lett sondrye sortes teares heretofore distilled behalfe youre discurtesye many dayes broughte end continuall sorow nyghtes drawen lengthe drayninge sighes ye present viewe pale ghastelye ghost perswade contrarye assurance vndowted loyaltie euer wherewith behelde without vente soddayne teares trycklynge alonge hys cheekes shee parte regarded earthe wyth face full dysdaine yt seamed whyche notwithstandynge construed proffitt hys sute pursewynge eftesones sorte ah madame haue hart deface glorie deuyne beautie wyth acte tyrrannie euer hath bene noted anye woman former tyme accompte yt vertue kyll hym dyethe euerye hower veray viewe remembrance heauenlye perfection wherein excell al euer haue bene called faire resolued haue ruyne stay executio abridge godd ladye lingringe torment presente dispatche ende lyfe deferr longer fatall minister wyl seynge aggreed performe effect suffer laste waterye eye stop streames auncient sorowe deryued onelye viewe remembrance mystrys contemplacions whereby harte shall also supp laste syropp desperate hope affection vanyshe dekaye bodye heare readie become fattall harbenger worlde hope reape hyer present merytt ladye whether anger woulde gyue longer place hys complaint dowted force charme ouerthrow fortresse chastetie gaue looke waspishe mynd reprehending rashnes theis suche like tearmes reproche yf pacience woulde yet giue leaue fonde discourse zilya repre hendeth vvoer see wante desyer attempte requestes neither parte preferr one condicion callynge yet honor brooke heare mouth suche soeke seduce honestie chaste lady wherein haue exacted vpon frendshipp facilitye vttermost sute presumyng belike consent depart wyth whiche restore againe besides present experience foule intent shall serue hereafter warraunte againste assaultes suche offer eyther selfe equal disposicto giue aunswere tearmes requeste fauor fowle attempte instant ceasse solicite eyther selfe embassador behalfe protestynge vnto part neyther seene streete place publike beinge longe countreye muche lesse suffer thaccesse anye gentleman within house onles bee neare parent allye whiche meanes importunity onely shall punishe wyth sorowful restrainte absence societie olde companion frendes whiche laste resolucion seamed suche mistery mynde thinfortunat virley time stoode enchaunted one newlye dropped fourth cloudes till laste one whollie conuerted dispaire fauor hande craued onelye consideracion paynes paste laste farewell loyall fayth kysse sayed sholde satisfye longynge full discharge pursewete accordynge requeste malicious ladye notinge fonde desyer knighte wyth small coste mighte nowe rydd importuante suter meanynge notwythstandyng departe small fauor price greate pennance hym soughte buy tolde hym aswell satisfye present request also make prooffe faith wolde performe full hys last demaunde yf wolde giue assurance sayth gentleman one thinge wherein require hym whiche simple vyrley onely promisse protestation religion othe pawned also maiestie highest performyng euery commandement pleased enioyne hym wherewith seamed satisfyed touchyng thassurance consent thervpon entred theffect owne promisse embracinge kissynge hym yf bene firste nighte theyr mariage requiryng hym like sorte become maister worde aduouche pointes late graunte pore gentleman suspectynge one thoughte suche tyrannye mistrys muche lesse shoulde buye kiss deare price tolde attended sommonee comaundement thende mighte witnes readye indeuor obeye enioyned hym hower till iij yeres expired shoulde become muett without speakynge sorte creature lyuing great euer occasion appeared true obseruynge whereof saith shall appeare experience faith whiche also maye force hereafter benefit contrarie wil discouer villante readye accuse periurie behalfe gentlewoman thinkes see perplexed countenaunce pore knighte hearinge sentence hard pennaunce iudged greate iniustice taxing cruell rate difficultie selfe performe theffect strage charge albeit hart greate papisticall performynge hys vowe began euen enter pointes commaundement declarynge signes bee obeyed wherewith gaue humble reuerence retyred immediatly hys lodgynge faygnynge suche aboute hym extremetie colde rhume distillynge partes braine taken awaye vse tounge domnes shoulde bee greeffe frendes moue disquiett demaundynge cause determyned bee straunger countrey till yeares pennaunce runne oute wherewith committynge order affayres mountcall el pyemount creditt suche thought meete supplye place suche truste tooke twoo three familyar companion assiste voyage whiche directed rightelye fraunce countreye moste meete hys abode chiefly mortall warres betwen charles seuenth valyaunt englishe men possessynge countrey yeare kynge campp gascoyne intent pursewe goodnes fortune delyuer contrey altogether thenglishe nacion addressed hymselfe force duchye normandye pyemountaine knight campp knowen diuerse chiefstaines aboute kynge aswell notable seruice seene hym diuerse place also greate creditt hathe afore wyth thearle pyemount became duke scauoye greate repaire nobilitye fraunce maryed madame iolante seconde doughter charles seuenth hadde whyle lamented lacke speache knowynge coulde doo cause suche disease presented hym afore maiestye wyth suche commendacyon hys vertue valyauntnes armes necessarye worthynes whyche forced greate lykynge kynge towardes hym alalbeit outwarde apparaunce argued infficiently inwarde dexteritie way whych also confyrmed pub licke view assalte kinge gaue english men within roan chiefe bool warke whole country normandy signeur philibarto gaue suche effecces forwardnes first seene vpon walles making waye souldiours enter breache towne wherein longe affore duke sommerset burned counterfait prophet fraunce called la pucelle leane whome pratinge frenchman affirme haue wrought merueiles armes warrs chiefly vnder conduite countryemen lost orleance wc diuerse holdes partes memory forged ydoll kepe yet amongest relikes abbay denys whych sawe may last great roostie sworde wherwith ashamed aduowche alogue de martuis hand buyried abbaye albeit saye rested foure tymes way haue founded iiii cross headles ymage saint denys holding stonye skalpe hande nowe oure dom philiberto whose forwardnes fortune faithe promised kepe without spot hys prince wher gaue good declaracion long skirmishe procured frenche agaynst englishe soldiours vnder guide onlye flower chyualrye tyme valyant captcine lorde talbot whose vertue made hym famons warrs verye remembrance hys name procureth terror stowtest frencheman thys daye lyueth ther skirmish may credit french bragge pyemontoyse talbot met vnhorssed eche wherupon kynge consideracion hys present seruice encrease corage contynue souldiour made hym capteyne diuerse holdes charge fyftie men armes wyth promisse word prince yt eafter shold find ample ner sorte prince oughte consider seruice suche whose vertue broughte soccours necessitie hym people wherein truely prince hath greate reason bestowe rewardes vpon deserue well embrase whyche carieth licknes hys owne nobylitie seinge vertue place soeuer shee take roote bring furthe good frutes vse effect wherof ought appeare vpon approche resemble place first seedes sowen neyther doth degree men according thopinion plyny deserue well hys prince souldiour whose woundes sayth inclosed sauetie whole countrey quiet seat royal neyther doth shrinke aduenture hys bodye agaynst thennemye establish reapose neyghbour hoame requite many daungers ye felde releue hys maymed lymmes cosumed wc ye warrs comittes hym hys retorne rigour iustice comonly wythout cause iust offence wherof think one contry christendom hable furnish many example miserie state englande god praysed hath benn greate occasion warr since happie raigne oure moste blessed quene nowe gouerneth lorde maiestie amend pitye see slenderly soldiours prouided tyranouslye persecuted malice caterpillors cyties franklinges countrye wherof wishe suche coulde name mooster mowthe trenche stande face breache thende might witnes daunger partaker perill warr doubt wolde force moste theim compassion touching souldiour also wolde defende beinge deuowred gallowes malice thus muche behalfe souldiours towardes wishe indiffrent care affore circumstance sondrie faltes chiefly reprehendinge greate wronge owne estimacion waye atteyne renowne vertue perillo repreheded cer teine fren de cleane contrary vicious pathe ydle playe wherein inuincible againste good councel made tractable hym plieth stronge loue stubborne vppon earthe men accomptes blindnes yt world vnsealed eye yougling tooke awaye vaile arrogante follie acknowledging euerie pointe wherein offende onely priuie owne falte also pertaker penance one poyson driueth oute one vice subiecte correctio falte soo inuincible ympression whyche poetes haue painted shape blynde boye properly called loue gamster onely forced spedye chaunge alteracion lyfe also sondrie sharpe shower aduersatie restored auncient entyer place honour estimacion instante within naples soiorned riche merchante blessed goddes handes chiefly faire vertuous doughter called carmosyna whose beautie made breach harte antonio perrillo graue admonicions thelders frendes albeit soo bewitched drowned nature lente younge man together bowntefull dispocition braue attyre courtlyke wearing apparell whyche one chyef allurement somons yt affection woman day found woman wil rather delite smal waste exterior pro porcion ymbrase vertue giftes comendacion man thoughte effect equal courtesie retorne affection semblable loue wherefore yf selte tormente passion nothynge inferior whiche also grewe exspectatio assurance promisse man must fele stynge thy infectio cause haue giuen imagin spoile mine honor imparte praye vnworthie euery waye iust comparison yf louynge conuenient thy inconstante dissemblinge disposition haue embased mine honor aduaunce thy renowme howe couldest thou without blushing attempte offer good hauing thy conscience poysened wyth many spotes abhominable traison howe whiche poetes call candle lightes goddesse loue bedd secrett louer solace mornyng resemblinge auncient delite enioyed ye presence mystres presented fresh allaram sorow recording eftesons vnhappie delite awake wyth heauenlye harmonye charme lytle birdes assurance enioye theffect whiche shadowe delitefull vision sprite presented theym night sleping greate contentemente vnhappie moste cruelly feloweship wilde bestes assiste tune complaintes ah venus whose starre heretofore hath onely guyded whose beames longe haue taken roote harte cause haue complaine thy iniustice whiche yeldes falshood faith tormente true constancie mynde hier loyaltie beareste thou tytle iuste pennance endure dischargeth name mercifull thou deale seuerly wyth thy true serseruantes kepest thou course amongest orient planettes heauen albeit yf abuselthy honor blasphemyng maiestie thy godheade sewe fauor seinge fele alredye ful weighte thy heauye hande neyther haste thou punishement store wherof taste force vnworthie affliction whiche seinge procedes thinfluence starr whiche gouerneth dispatche messenger thy determinacion thende death distresse may receiue ende cruell mistres performe glorious triumphe victorye pynynge lyfe complaintes coulde staye swifte course tyme ware heighte son showed declining daye whiche moued hym increase pase leauing common wayes folowe pathes leaste acquainted traueile wherein continued withoute intermission till cloasinge euenyng wearynes horsses forced theim discend take harbor within litle village farre ordinary waye whence litle releeff horsses lesse rest theim selues departed wandring sorte space three foure dayes nightes thende whereof broughte theim laste foote large mountaine inhabited onely sauage beastes creature vnreasonable discoueringe rounde platt soile pleasame prospecte moste proper shroode solitarie life wandrynge knyghte delyted shade hadd benefytt nomber pleasante tree whiche nature seamed lende hym speciall solace wyldernes sorowe desyered vse open prospecte plaine forrestes chase wyth theyr wholle heardes deare fortes offred giue hym skoape recorde greeffe chaunge recreation mighte viewe hideus highe rockes whose steepnes craggie scituation albeit moued terrour beholder yet without cause greate delite reason pleasant grene garnished tappissery diuerse flower spreadyng theim selues onge heighte sayde mountes whiche moued moste affection place merueilous faire rowmey caue enuironed side beeche cypre pyneaple ceder tree wyth braunches yeldynge frutes diuerse kindes righte afore mouth openyng tendyng valley appered nomber pleasante graftes whose rootes receiuing moisture cleare streame passing wyth softe noyse alonge dore caue gaue suche bountifull norryture twigges tender branch thonly topps bowed downe dipped theim selues vppon dutie fountaine wonderfull clearenes fedyng continuallye saide streame whiche seamed offer suche solace solytarye intent diego without aduise determined performe penance wente doo conuerte house builded nature monasterye profession wherein mente ende voyage deuocions commandynge man alight vnsadlinge horse gaue theim keye wilde forestes whereof hetherto harde newes touchinge saddells harnesse furniture horsses bestowed within litle cell corner caue also leauing ordinarye apparell putt theyr habittes pilgrim man made prouision accordynge condicion state necessitye place dyggynge firste indeuor certeine soddes lomppes claye wherewith entrenched rampierd felden shopp defende theym againste furye wilde beastes otherwayes myghte oppresse theym nyghte made also twoo beddes lytle couch softe mosse wyth testure side wodde hewde lesse fyne proporcion yf skill carpenter assisted worke hadd releeffe foode longe tyme frute whiche wilde tree yelde theym one lesse sometime chaunge dyot gladd feede rawe rootes whiche digged thintrailles earth vntill extreme hunger preferred meane supplie thinne fare whiche man made crosbowe whiche killed often time hare conie fedynge releeff time beguiled wilde goate mountaines often bane greater beaste forreste whose blood pressed betwene twoo peces woode made nonst deuidynge theim morsells whiche rosted wyth heatte son furnished sober manner leane table disgestynge theyr rude vnholsome dyelt wyth cuppe colde water whereof lesse plentye charge commaunded ouer whole cellers delicate wyne pallayes dom diego increased dweile presente miserye wyth teares continuall complainte inueighynge againste malice fortune wherein vsed common exercise walke alone moste daungerous place desertes enterteynyng solytarye thoughtes sende pleasante calme stormye tempest whiche kepes hym anker amongest perillous rockes pireneus enformed conuenient meane ease distresse languishinge frend fedd hope promise failed add assured effect vppon first hower midnighte olde ladye seruantes ouerwhelmed wyth charme mantel dead slepe least apte suspect conspiracy determyned depart castell mistres parte furnished wantes necessaryes touchinge voyage hastie resolucion required spedie diligence knight hys parte also vsed lesse expedicion conuenient beynge come hys house caused arme ten xy gentleman hys neyghbours vassalls communicated hys intente night two three howers affore departure biskayne hys companye marched secret maner directly waye sholde passe til came groue coppyes younge woode regardinge highe way one side mayne common plaine thother syde bestowinge himselfe company bushe harde yinediatly noyse horsses men approching vnfortunate diligence lighte moone discouered gentlewoman whose bewtie seamed contende brightnes nexte vnto ridd miserable louer whome assone roderico parceiued within daunger carear felt conuersion aunciente anger compassion presente furye whose force sommonynge hym effect morder caused hym saieth worthie honor knightehodd thou hast forfeited thy faith geniuera exclameth roderico detestable traison vpon thou oughtest wreake effecte thy malicious villanye hast thou dissembled thy grudge longe showe fliering fauor like cockadrell towardes house vomitt thy venim vpon neuer deserued wel thy handes haste thou face intreate seinge presence thou hast killed whose blood wil purse vpo thine longe haue one gaspe breath accuse thy villanie authoritye hast thou inquire doinges impesh determination sorte bound yelde ye accopte resolution mine hath made arbitrator much lesse giuen comission debate vpo tharticles mariage onlesse thy malice force loue desloyall villaine thou haste comitted acte perpetuall infamie thy name whereof also part wil reserue remebrance storehouse hart death shal take awaie ye desier reuenge wrong thou hast done albeit fortune hath made thy prisoner power dispose thy pleasure yet haue one resistance defeate extremitie thy force also wil faile put execution yt afore thy traiterous cliate diego quenche thurste wt precious iewste virginitie theis hades readie giue fatal pasport visit bloodie ghoste loyaltie thou hast slain traiterous cospiracie therfore maye histo fol disordered lyfe countesse celant lyuynge long adulterie procured diuerse morders receyued hyer wickednes shamefull death histo fol ivlya drowneth selfe bodye abused force histo fol impudent loue ladye chabrie procurer tolonyo together detestable morders committed betwene theim histo fol lvchin longe loue wyth simple maide woeth wyn anye passion endureth laste necessitie yeldeth handes dothe onelye refuce abuse bodie also take order susteine supplie wantes lesse amplie yf bene syster histo fol crueltye wydowe enioynynge woer pennance thre yeres losse speeche folishe loyaltye hym
